<P>meruzULa badha antareNa kathA

<P>AraNyaka parba sadA saMpUrNNa bAratA | 1 |

<P>y1ethu antare birATa parba kathA

<P>kahasi maharuSi tumbhe paNDita bhigyaMbantA | 2 |

<P>meruzULa badhakari pANDaba pan~chubIre

<P>byAsa marakaNDa bAlamIka munibare | 3 |

<P>bahuta kalyANa bAn~cchA kale arjunaku

<P>tuhi se tapIbaLa nizcaLa kalu ye AmbhaMku | 4 |

<P>aneka dAnabe ye thile y1ehu bane

<P>samaste nAzagale y1ekA tohora prasanme | 5 |

<P>kimbhIrI kinnarI Adi baka hiDimbeka

<P>pANDabAsura rebAsura Au hiraNeka | 6 |

<P>moDhAsura kalpAsura japAsura nirbAta kapaca

<P>kumbha nikumbha Abara goSiMha kALin~cha | 7 |

<P1>4|2 tuhi se tapa nirmaLakalu AmbhaMku |--Na, Ta, gha, n~ja

<P>prohite boile ho bara Asu y1ebe

<P>caLanti Dagara ye abhimanyu ThAbe | 325 |

<P>arjyUna kumAra ye dibya beza hoi

<P>berIra madhye bije karAile nei | 326 |

<P>ki abA airAbrata teji Asai surapati | 327 |

<P>ki abA rati tejyA kari ailA anaGga

<P>hAra niALI padaka tADa ye toDhara

<P>aneka ratna AbharaNa tAhAra zarIra | 329 |

<P>guru debatAMku namaskAra kari

<P>bijekalA kunara dadhi maMgaLa sumari | 330 |

[MBO-05-676]

<P>samasta brAhmaNe ye kaleka bedadhuni

<P>prohita abhamukhe samasta mahAmuni | 336 |

[MBO-05-677]

<P>bhISma dhrutiraSTra bidura an~jay1e pAn~chALa deza ray1e

<P>pAn~chapANDaba ye samasta rAjA kuMkumamay1e | 349 |

<P>bhojanara sampada kahite ki pAri
